# Program name:	Makefile
# Description:	Build the conformance examples distribution
# Author:	Don Brutzman NPS and Mike Kass NIST
# Revised:	29 January 2001
# Invocation:	make all

# - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -

TRANSLATION_DRIVE	= C:

TRANSLATION_DIR		= www.web3D.org/TaskGroups/x3d/translation

XMLINT_LOCATION		= c:/xml/microsoft

# - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -

all:
#	make -i wrap
#	make -i unwrap
	make -i models
	make -i pages
	make -i ConformancePages
	make -i compress-all


ConformancePages:
	cd ../../dom; pwd;	javac Filter*.java
	cd ../../dom; pwd;	javac ReferenceDocumentationLayout.java
	cd ../../dom; pwd;	java  ReferenceDocumentationLayout -sections ../examples/Conformance/
	ls -l ChapterLayout.xml
	cat   ChapterLayout.xml
	@echo create web pages
	"$(TRANSLATION_DRIVE)/$(TRANSLATION_DIR)/saxon.bat"  -t  ChapterLayout.xml  $(TRANSLATION_DRIVE)/$(TRANSLATION_DIR)/dom/LayoutReferenceChaptersPages.xsl
#	xmlint must be last
	pwd; $(XMLINT_LOCATION)/xmlint ChapterLayout.xml

compress:
	make -i compress-all

compress-all:
	@echo 'Delete PFE ."$$$$$$" backup files:'
#	       ($$ => $ in bash shell)
	rm -f  *.'$$$$$$'
	rm -f  */*.'$$$$$$'
	rm -f  */*/*.'$$$$$$'
	rm -f  */*/*/*.'$$$$$$'
	rm -f  _new_result.wrl
	rm -f  */_new_result.wrl
	rm -f  */*/_new_result.wrl
	rm -f  */*/*/_new_result.wrl
	cd ../../../../../../;	jar -cvf     ConformanceExamples.zip www.web3D.org/TaskGroups/x3d/translation/examples/Conformance/*
	mv ../../../../../../ConformanceExamples.zip ../../
	ls -al   ../../ConformanceExamples.zip

next:
	@echo -------------------------------------------------------------------------
	pwd; $(XMLINT_LOCATION)/xmlint 'Appearance\Appearance\imagetexture.xml'
	$(TRANSLATION_DRIVE)/$(TRANSLATION_DIR)/X3dUnwrap.bat   'Appearance\Appearance\imagetexture'				-same
	$(TRANSLATION_DRIVE)/$(TRANSLATION_DIR)/X3dToVrml97.bat 'Appearance\Appearance\imagetexture'				-same
	$(TRANSLATION_DRIVE)/$(TRANSLATION_DIR)/X3dToHtml.bat   'Appearance\Appearance\imagetexture'				-same
